msg:The hotel is newly opened in 2023. The high floors are between the 35th and 40th floors. The rooms are quite large and there is a laundry room and a gym. Downstairs is the KK Time shopping mall.

The hotel is otherwise good, but it has two fatal shortcomings:
1) The sound insulation is extremely poor - I was woken up by neighbors several times while sleeping. You can hear the neighbors opening and closing doors, and they are very loud. If the door is not closed properly, a loud alarm will sound. You can hear your neighbors if they speak loudly or turn on the TV.
2) Wifi is sometimes good and bad - when it is bad, you can't watch videos normally and can only read text. Photos and videos cannot be sent either.

All in all, it was a very annoying stay and I won't come back again.
